PRO FEATURES ADDED TO FREE BLOCKS\n\n### A. Block Conditions (Visibility Rules)\n**File:** `/inc/plugins/class-block-conditions.php`\n\nAdds conditional visibility to ANY block with 14+ condition types:\n\n**User-Based Conditions:**\n- `loggedInUserMeta` - Check logged-in user meta values\n- `postMeta` - Check post meta conditions\n- `country` - Geo-targeting based on user location\n- `queryString` - URL parameter matching\n- `cookie` - Browser cookie values\n\n**Date/Time Conditions:**\n- `dateRange` - Specific date range visibility (start_date check)\n- `dateRecurring` - Recurring on specific days of week\n- `timeRecurring` - Recurring time windows (daily)\n\n**WooCommerce-Specific Conditions:**\n- `wooProductsInCart` - Show if products in cart\n- `wooTotalCartValue` - Show if cart total > X amount\n- `wooPurchaseHistory` - Show if user bought products\n- `wooTotalSpent` - Show if lifetime spend > X\n- `wooCategory` - Show if browsing product category\n- `wooTag` - Show if browsing product tag\n- `wooAttribute` - Show if product has attribute\n\n**LearnDash Integration Conditions:**\n- `learnDashPurchaseHistory` - Course purchase status\n- `learnDashCourseStatus` - Course completion tracking\n\n### B. Dynamic Content Tags\n**File:** `/inc/plugins/class-dynamic-content.php`\n\nEnables dynamic content population via filters:\n- `otter_blocks_evaluate_dynamic_content_text` - Text field values\n- `otter_blocks_evaluate_dynamic_content_link` - Link URLs\n- `otter_blocks_evaluate_dynamic_content_media_server` - Media server resources\n- `otter_blocks_evaluate_dynamic_content_media_content` - Media content\n\n**Supported Dynamic Sources:**\n- Post date/time formatting\n- Post terms (categories, tags)\n- Post meta fields\n- ACF (Advanced Custom Fields) integration\n- Author meta\n- Logged-in user meta\n- Query string parameters\n- Client IP & Country detection\n- WooCommerce product data\n- ACF field values (text, URL, media)\n\n### C. ARCHITECTURE & INTEGRATION MODEL\n\n### How Pro Extends Free\n\n**Entry Point:** `/otter-pro.php` (lines 138-150)\n```php\nadd_action('plugins_loaded', function() {\n    if (function_exists('register_block_type') && \n        defined('OTTER_BLOCKS_VERSION') && \n        defined('OTTER_BLOCKS_PRO_SUPPORT')) {\n        require_once __DIR__ .
